**Code changes this session (src/):** ONE commit `81728ec` (1242 insertions, 52 deletions across 4 src files; 1 new + 2 modified):

- `src/app/projects/[projectId]/competition-scraping/components/ColumnFilters.tsx` (NEW) — popover shell with outside-click + Esc dismiss + 3 filter primitives + URL-query serialization helpers + pure row filter + option-list helper. `MultiSelectFilter` renders a checkbox list over the platform-scoped distinct values + a "(blank)" pseudo-row when at least one row is null/blank + a search-within-list input when option count > 6 + Apply/Clear footer. `NumericRangeFilter` renders min/max number inputs with HTML-native step + range validation + "Min must be ≤ Max" inline error. `DateRangeFilter` renders from/to YYYY-MM-DD inputs with format + range validation. `readFiltersFromQuery` / `writeFiltersToQuery` round-trip filter state through URLSearchParams using repeated keys for multi-select with `__blank__` token + single keys for ranges. Pure `applyColumnFilters(rows, filters)` returns the filtered subset. `computeDistinctValues(rows)` returns the case-insensitive-sorted distinct values for the 3 vocabulary cols. `EMPTY_COLUMN_FILTERS` constant + `isColumnFilterActive` / `countActiveColumnFilters` introspection helpers.
- `src/app/projects/[projectId]/competition-scraping/components/UrlTable.tsx` (modified) — accepts new `filters`/`onFiltersChange`/`scopeRows` props; computes distinct values + has-blank-row signals from `scopeRows`; column filters apply BEFORE sort. Each filterable `<th>` now renders a sort label-button alongside a funnel-icon trigger; clicking the label still toggles sort per slice (a.1) behavior, clicking the funnel opens that column's filter popover. Funnel turns blue with a small dot when filter active. New "Clear all filters (N active)" toolbar button shows only when ≥ 1 filter is set. "Showing N of M" reflects all active filters.
- `src/app/projects/[projectId]/competition-scraping/components/CompetitionScrapingViewer.tsx` (modified) — filter state derived from URL query each render via `readFiltersFromQuery` so back/forward and deep-links round-trip; `handleFiltersChange` calls `router.replace` with `writeFiltersToQuery`-mutated params. `scopeRows` passed to UrlTable so multi-select option lists derive from the platform-scoped row set NOT search-narrowed (other filters don't shrink the available options). New `?q=` for free-text search box with 250ms debounce write — local `draftSearch` mirror updates instantly while a useEffect schedules the URL write; back/forward syncs the draft from the URL.

**Verification at end-of-session:** 393/393 src/lib tests pass (no test changes — pure UI work; no `src/lib` surface touched); tsc clean (`npx tsc --noEmit`); build clean (49 routes; same as slice (a.3) — zero new API routes); lint reports 13 errors / 39 warnings project-wide at exact baseline parity with slice (a.3) — the 13 errors all live in pre-existing files outside the W#2 surface (`think-tank/page.tsx` Date.now() purity, `keyword-clustering/components/TVTTable.tsx`, `MTTable.tsx`, etc.) — AND `npx eslint src/app/projects/\[projectId\]/competition-scraping/components/ColumnFilters.tsx ...UrlTable.tsx ...CompetitionScrapingViewer.tsx` reports clean (zero errors, zero warnings on the 3 slice (a.4) files).

## Document lifecycle management (reference)

Per `DOCUMENTATION_ARCHITECTURE.md` §5 (Tool Graduation Ritual):
- Group B docs have three states: **Active development** → **Graduated** → **Archived**
- Graduation splits the doc into `<TOOL>_ARCHIVE.md` (full history) + `<TOOL>_DATA_CONTRACT.md` (what downstream tools need to know)
- Trigger for graduation: tool is production-stable AND a downstream tool needs to consume its data

Per `DOCUMENTATION_ARCHITECTURE.md` §2 (Group system):
- Group A is system-wide; always uploaded
- Group B is tool-specific; uploaded when the chat's scope includes that tool
- Group C is optional reference material

Per `HANDOFF_PROTOCOL.md` Document Update Checklist (end-of-chat):
- Checks 11 conditions; updates are triggered when conditions match
- Always-updated: CHAT_REGISTRY, NEW_CHAT_PROMPT, DOCUMENT_MANIFEST (ran this chat ✅)
- CORRECTIONS_LOG updated when mistakes occurred this chat (ran this chat ✅ — Pattern 11 4th-recurrence entry + Option A leftover-handling procedural entry + methodology-shift decision entry all added)
- Navigation/routes updated when routes changed (ran this chat ✅ — NAVIGATION_MAP + PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE updated for `/dashboard/notes`, `/plos/notes`, `/plos` KC-card rewire)
- Roadmap updated when a roadmap item completed (ran this chat ✅ — Ckpt 8 marked complete; Ckpt 9 scope expanded to include `/docs/` setup; Claude Code migration added as top-priority post-Ckpt-9 item)
- Tool-specific doc updated when tool changed (ran this chat ✅ — KEYWORD_CLUSTERING_ACTIVE updated for `/plos` navigation-path fix)
- Protocol docs updated for methodology shift (ran this chat ✅ — HANDOFF_PROTOCOL §9 added for Claude Code; DOCUMENTATION_ARCHITECTURE §15 added for doc-system evolution)
- New docs created (ran this chat ✅ — CLAUDE_CODE_MIGRATION.md as Group A #13; CLAUDE_CODE_STARTER.md as non-Group-A operational file)
